Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Database.Command:Information: Executed DbCommand (35ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT TOP(1) COUNT(*) AS [CountOrders], SUM([t].[OrderShippingExclTax]) AS [SumShippingExclTax], SUM([t].[PaymentMethodAdditionalFeeExclTax]) AS [OrderPaymentFeeExclTaxSum], SUM([t].[OrderTax]) AS [SumTax], SUM([t].[OrderTotal]) AS [SumOrders], SUM([t].[RefundedAmount]) AS [SumRefundedAmount]
FROM (
    SELECT [o].*, 1 AS [Key]
    FROM [Order] AS [o]
    WHERE ([o].[Deleted] = 0) AND [o].[OrderStatusId] IN (40)
) AS [t]
GROUP BY [t].[Key]
